src/server.js:688:
src/server.js:689:// OAuth 2.0 with PKCE - Start authentication flow
src/server.js:690:// User must be logged in with GitHub first
src/server.js:691:app.get('/auth/x', async (req, res) => {
src/server.js:692:  try {
src/server.js:693:    // Get GitHub user from cookie - required for per-user X OAuth
src/server.js:694:    const githubUserId = getGithubUserIdFromCookie(req);
src/server.js:695:    if (!githubUserId) {
src/server.js:696:      return res.send(renderXAuthPage({
src/server.js:697:        title: 'GitHub login required',
src/server.js:698:        message: 'Please sign in with GitHub before connecting your X account.',
src/server.js:699:        detail: 'X accounts are linked to your GitHub account for multi-user support.',
src/server.js:700:        status: 'error'
src/server.js:701:      }));
src/server.js:702:    }
src/server.js:703:    
src/server.js:704:    const oauthHandler = new OAuthHandler();
src/server.js:705:    const { authUrl, codeVerifier } = oauthHandler.generateAuthUrl();
src/server.js:706:    
src/server.js:707:    // Generate a unique state to prevent CSRF and store with user info
src/server.js:708:    const state = `x_${Date.now()}_${githubUserId}`;
src/server.js:709:    
src/server.js:710:    // Store PKCE verifier with GitHub user ID for callback
src/server.js:711:    pkceStore.set(state, {
src/server.js:712:      codeVerifier,
src/server.js:713:      githubUserId,
src/server.js:714:      timestamp: Date.now()
src/server.js:715:    });
src/server.js:716:    
src/server.js:717:    // Clean up old PKCE states (older than 10 minutes)
src/server.js:718:    const tenMinutesAgo = Date.now() - 10 * 60 * 1000;
src/server.js:719:    for (const [key, value] of pkceStore.entries()) {
src/server.js:720:      if (value.timestamp && value.timestamp < tenMinutesAgo) {
src/server.js:721:        pkceStore.delete(key);
src/server.js:722:      }
src/server.js:723:    }
src/server.js:724:    
src/server.js:725:    // Modify auth URL to use our custom state
src/server.js:726:    const authUrlWithState = authUrl.replace(/state=[^&]+/, `state=${encodeURIComponent(state)}`);
src/server.js:727:    
src/server.js:728:    console.log(`🔐 Starting X OAuth for GitHub user: ${githubUserId}`);
src/server.js:729:    res.redirect(authUrlWithState);
src/server.js:730:  } catch (error) {
src/server.js:731:    console.error('❌ X OAuth initialization error:', error);
src/server.js:732:    res
src/server.js:733:      .status(500)
src/server.js:734:      .send(renderXAuthPage({
src/server.js:735:        title: 'X OAuth initialization failed',
src/server.js:736:        message: 'We could not start the X connection flow. Please try again in a moment.',
src/server.js:737:        detail: `Error: ${error.message}. Make sure OAUTH_CLIENT_ID is set.`,
src/server.js:738:        status: 'error'
src/server.js:739:      }));
src/server.js:740:  }
src/server.js:741:});
src/server.js:742:
src/server.js:743:// X OAuth callback with PKCE (per-user)
src/server.js:744:app.get('/auth/x/callback', async (req, res) => {
src/server.js:745:  const { code, error, error_description, state } = req.query;
src/server.js:746:  
src/server.js:747:  if (error) {
src/server.js:748:    console.error('❌ X OAuth Error:', error);
src/server.js:749:    res.send(renderXAuthPage({
src/server.js:750:      title: 'X authorization failed',
src/server.js:751:      message: 'We did not receive authorization from X.',
src/server.js:752:      detail: `Error: ${error}${error_description ? `. ${error_description}` : ''}`,
src/server.js:753:      status: 'error'
src/server.js:754:    }));
src/server.js:755:    return;
src/server.js:756:  }
src/server.js:757:
src/server.js:758:  if (!code) {
src/server.js:759:    res.status(400).send('No authorization code received');
src/server.js:760:    return;
src/server.js:761:  }
src/server.js:762:
src/server.js:763:  try {
src/server.js:764:    // Get stored PKCE data including GitHub user ID
src/server.js:765:    const pkceData = pkceStore.get(state);
src/server.js:766:    if (!pkceData || !pkceData.codeVerifier) {
src/server.js:767:      throw new Error('PKCE code verifier not found. Please restart the OAuth flow.');
src/server.js:768:    }
src/server.js:769:    
src/server.js:770:    const { codeVerifier, githubUserId } = pkceData;
src/server.js:771:    
src/server.js:772:    if (!githubUserId) {
src/server.js:773:      throw new Error('GitHub user ID not found. Please sign in with GitHub first.');
src/server.js:774:    }
src/server.js:775:    
src/server.js:776:    // Get the X OAuth user ID for this GitHub user
src/server.js:777:    const xOAuthUserId = database.getXOAuthUserId(githubUserId);
src/server.js:778:    
src/server.js:779:    const oauthHandler = new OAuthHandler();
src/server.js:780:    await oauthHandler.exchangeCodeForTokens(code, codeVerifier, xOAuthUserId);
src/server.js:781:    
src/server.js:782:    pkceStore.delete(state);
src/server.js:783:    
src/server.js:784:    console.log(`✅ X account connected for GitHub user: ${githubUserId} (stored as: ${xOAuthUserId})`);
src/server.js:785:    
src/server.js:786:    res.send(renderXAuthPage({
src/server.js:787:      title: 'X connected successfully',
src/server.js:788:      message: 'Your X account is now linked to your GitLogs account.',
src/server.js:789:      detail: 'Your X connection is personal and won\'t affect other users. You can safely close this window.',
src/server.js:790:      status: 'success'
src/server.js:791:    }));
src/server.js:792:  } catch (error) {
src/server.js:793:    console.error('❌ X Token exchange error:', error);
src/server.js:794:    res
src/server.js:795:      .status(500)
src/server.js:796:      .send(renderXAuthPage({
src/server.js:797:        title: 'X token exchange failed',
src/server.js:798:        message: 'We could not finish the X connection.',
src/server.js:799:        detail: `Error: ${error.message}`,
src/server.js:800:        status: 'error'
src/server.js:801:      }));
src/server.js:802:  }
src/server.js:803:});
src/server.js:804:

src/server.js:841:  
src/server.js:842:  if (!adminKey) {
src/server.js:843:    if (config.server.nodeEnv === 'development') {
src/server.js:844:      return next();
src/server.js:845:    }
src/server.js:846:    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Admin API not configured' });
src/server.js:847:  }
src/server.js:848:  
src/server.js:849:  if (apiKey !== adminKey) {
src/server.js:850:    return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid API key' });
src/server.js:851:  }
src/server.js:852:  
src/server.js:853:  next();
src/server.js:854:}

src/server.js:1177:  async function gracefulShutdown(signal) {
src/server.js:1178:    if (isShuttingDown) {
src/server.js:1179:      console.log('⚠️  Shutdown already in progress...');
src/server.js:1180:      return;
src/server.js:1181:    }
src/server.js:1182:
src/server.js:1183:    isShuttingDown = true;
src/server.js:1184:    console.log(`\n🛑 Received ${signal}, starting graceful shutdown...`);
src/server.js:1185:
src/server.js:1186:    // Stop accepting new connections
src/server.js:1187:    server.close((err) => {
src/server.js:1188:      if (err) {
src/server.js:1189:        console.error('❌ Error closing server:', err.message);
src/server.js:1190:      } else {
src/server.js:1191:        console.log('✅ Server closed - no new connections');
src/server.js:1192:      }
src/server.js:1193:    });
src/server.js:1194:
src/server.js:1195:    try {
src/server.js:1196:      // Stop queue service (persists pending items)
src/server.js:1197:      console.log('💾 Stopping queue service...');
src/server.js:1198:      shutdownQueueService();

src/server.js:1200:      // Close database connection (saves and closes)

src/server.js:1202:      database.closeDatabase();
src/server.js:1203:
src/server.js:1204:      console.log('✅ Graceful shutdown complete');
src/server.js:1205:      process.exit(0);
src/server.js:1206:    } catch (error) {
src/server.js:1207:      console.error('❌ Error during shutdown:', error.message);
src/server.js:1208:      process.exit(1);
src/server.js:1209:    }
src/server.js:1210:  }

src/server.js:1213:  process.on('SIGTERM', () => gracefulShutdown('SIGTERM'));

src/webhookHandler.js:11:/**
src/webhookHandler.js:12: * Verify GitHub webhook signature
src/webhookHandler.js:13: * Supports both global secret and per-repository secrets (multi-user)
src/webhookHandler.js:14: * 
src/webhookHandler.js:15: * @param {string} payload - Raw request body as string
src/webhookHandler.js:16: * @param {string} signature - X-Hub-Signature-256 header value
src/webhookHandler.js:17: * @param {string} repoFullName - Repository full name for per-repo secrets
src/webhookHandler.js:18: * @returns {boolean} - True if signature is valid
src/webhookHandler.js:19: */
src/webhookHandler.js:20:function verifyGitHubSignature(payload, signature, repoFullName = null) {
src/webhookHandler.js:21:  // Try per-repository secret first (multi-user support)
src/webhookHandler.js:22:  let secret = null;
src/webhookHandler.js:23:  if (repoFullName) {
src/webhookHandler.js:24:    secret = database.getRepoWebhookSecret(repoFullName);
src/webhookHandler.js:25:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:26:  
src/webhookHandler.js:27:  // Fall back to global secret
src/webhookHandler.js:28:  if (!secret) {
src/webhookHandler.js:29:    secret = config.github.webhookSecret;
src/webhookHandler.js:30:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:31:  
src/webhookHandler.js:32:  if (!secret) {
src/webhookHandler.js:33:    // Fail CLOSED: with no secret we cannot authenticate the sender, so we must
src/webhookHandler.js:34:    // reject rather than accept forged push events. A misconfigured server that
src/webhookHandler.js:35:    // rejects all webhooks is loud and safe; one that accepts everything is not.
src/webhookHandler.js:36:    console.error(
src/webhookHandler.js:37:      '❌ No webhook secret configured (per-repo or global WEBHOOK_SECRET). ' +
src/webhookHandler.js:38:        'Rejecting webhook — cannot verify signature.'
src/webhookHandler.js:39:    );
src/webhookHandler.js:40:    return false;
src/webhookHandler.js:41:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:42:
src/webhookHandler.js:43:  if (!signature) {
src/webhookHandler.js:44:    console.error('❌ No signature provided in request');
src/webhookHandler.js:45:    return false;
src/webhookHandler.js:46:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:47:
src/webhookHandler.js:48:  const hmac = crypto.createHmac('sha256', secret);
src/webhookHandler.js:49:  const digest = 'sha256=' + hmac.update(payload).digest('hex');
src/webhookHandler.js:50:  try {
src/webhookHandler.js:51:    return crypto.timingSafeEqual(
src/webhookHandler.js:52:      Buffer.from(signature),
src/webhookHandler.js:53:      Buffer.from(digest)
src/webhookHandler.js:54:    );
src/webhookHandler.js:55:  } catch (err) {
src/webhookHandler.js:56:    return false;
src/webhookHandler.js:57:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:58:}
src/webhookHandler.js:59:
src/webhookHandler.js:60:/**
src/webhookHandler.js:61: * Check if repository is allowed and enabled for posting (supports multi-user)
src/webhookHandler.js:62: */
src/webhookHandler.js:63:function isRepoAllowed(repoFullName) {
src/webhookHandler.js:64:  // First check if repo is enabled by any user
src/webhookHandler.js:65:  const isEnabled = database.isRepoEnabled(repoFullName);
src/webhookHandler.js:66:  console.log(`🔍 Checking repo ${repoFullName}: isRepoEnabled=${isEnabled}`);
src/webhookHandler.js:67:  
src/webhookHandler.js:68:  if (isEnabled) {
src/webhookHandler.js:69:    return true;
src/webhookHandler.js:70:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:71:  
src/webhookHandler.js:72:  // Fall back to global allowed repos list (for legacy/admin use)
src/webhookHandler.js:73:  if (!config.github.allowedRepos) {
src/webhookHandler.js:74:    console.log(`⚠️  Repo ${repoFullName} not enabled in DB and no ALLOWED_REPOS configured`);
src/webhookHandler.js:75:    return false; // No global list and not enabled by user = not allowed
src/webhookHandler.js:76:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:77:  
src/webhookHandler.js:78:  const inAllowedList = config.github.allowedRepos.includes(repoFullName);
src/webhookHandler.js:79:  console.log(`🔍 Checking ALLOWED_REPOS for ${repoFullName}: inList=${inAllowedList}`);
src/webhookHandler.js:80:  return inAllowedList;
src/webhookHandler.js:81:}
src/webhookHandler.js:82:
src/webhookHandler.js:83:/**
src/webhookHandler.js:84: * Get or generate repository context

src/webhookHandler.js:86: */
src/webhookHandler.js:87:async function getOrGenerateRepoContext(repository, commits = []) {
src/webhookHandler.js:88:  const repoFullName = repository.full_name;
src/webhookHandler.js:89:  
src/webhookHandler.js:90:  // Check cache first
src/webhookHandler.js:91:  if (!database.isRepoContextStale(repoFullName, 24)) {
src/webhookHandler.js:92:    const cached = database.getRepoContext(repoFullName);
src/webhookHandler.js:93:    if (cached) {
src/webhookHandler.js:94:      console.log(`📦 Using cached repo context for: ${repoFullName}`);
src/webhookHandler.js:95:      return cached;
src/webhookHandler.js:96:    }
src/webhookHandler.js:97:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:98:

src/webhookHandler.js:100:  console.log(`🔍 Generating repo context for: ${repoFullName}`);
src/webhookHandler.js:101:  const context = repoIndexer.generateContextFromWebhook(repository, commits);
src/webhookHandler.js:102:

src/webhookHandler.js:105:

src/webhookHandler.js:107:}

src/webhookHandler.js:109:function isMergeCommit(commit) {
src/webhookHandler.js:110:  // Check if commit message indicates a merge
src/webhookHandler.js:111:  const message = commit.message || '';
src/webhookHandler.js:112:  const mergePatterns = [
src/webhookHandler.js:113:    /^Merge branch/i,
src/webhookHandler.js:114:    /^Merge pull request/i,
src/webhookHandler.js:115:    /^Merge .+ into/i,
src/webhookHandler.js:116:    /^Merged .+ into/i
src/webhookHandler.js:117:  ];
src/webhookHandler.js:118:  
src/webhookHandler.js:119:  // Check message patterns
src/webhookHandler.js:120:  if (mergePatterns.some(pattern => pattern.test(message))) {
src/webhookHandler.js:121:    return true;
src/webhookHandler.js:122:  }
src/webhookHandler.js:123:  
src/webhookHandler.js:124:  // Check if commit has multiple parents (merge commit)
src/webhookHandler.js:125:  // Note: GitHub webhook doesn't always include parent info, so we rely on message
src/webhookHandler.js:126:  return false;
src/webhookHandler.js:127:}
src/webhookHandler.js:128:
src/webhookHandler.js:129:/**
src/webhookHandler.js:130: * Process a single commit with enhanced context
src/webhookHandler.js:131: * Now uses two-stage AI generation for accurate changelogs
src/webhookHandler.js:132: * 
src/webhookHandler.js:133: * @param {object} commit - Git commit object
src/webhookHandler.js:134: * @param {object} repository - Repository information
src/webhookHandler.js:135: * @param {object} pusher - Pusher information
src/webhookHandler.js:136: * @param {object} options - Additional options (repoContext, userId, xOAuthUserId, githubUserId)
src/webhookHandler.js:137: */
src/webhookHandler.js:138:async function processCommit(commit, repository, pusher, options = {}) {
src/webhookHandler.js:139:  const { repoContext = null, userId = 'default', xOAuthUserId = 'default', githubUserId = null } = options;
src/webhookHandler.js:140:  
src/webhookHandler.js:141:  try {
src/webhookHandler.js:142:    console.log(`📝 Processing commit: ${commit.id.substring(0, 7)} (user: ${userId}, xAuth: ${xOAuthUserId})`);
src/webhookHandler.js:143:
src/webhookHandler.js:144:    // Idempotency: GitHub re-delivers webhooks. Skip commits already tweeted so
src/webhookHandler.js:145:    // a redelivery never double-posts (the post→persist order can't dedup after
src/webhookHandler.js:146:    // the fact). Cheap check before any AI/network work.
src/webhookHandler.js:147:    if (config.database.enabled) {
src/webhookHandler.js:148:      const alreadyTweeted = await database.getTweetsForRepo(repository.full_name);
src/webhookHandler.js:149:      if (alreadyTweeted.some((t) => t.commit_sha === commit.id)) {
src/webhookHandler.js:150:        console.log(`⏭️  Commit ${commit.id.substring(0, 7)} already tweeted — skipping (idempotent)`);
src/webhookHandler.js:151:        return { success: true, skipped: true };
src/webhookHandler.js:152:      }
src/webhookHandler.js:153:    }
src/webhookHandler.js:154:
src/webhookHandler.js:155:    const commitData = commitFormatter.formatCommit(commit, repository, pusher);
src/webhookHandler.js:156:
src/webhookHandler.js:157:    // Check if user is using the default template (for formatting decisions)

docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:62:    WH->>WH: HMAC-SHA256(rawBody) compared via timingSafeEqual
docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:257:- **HMAC fails OPEN when no secret is configured.** `verifyGitHubSignature` returns `true` (and only logs a warning) if neither a per-repo secret nor `WEBHOOK_SECRET` is set (`webhookHandler.js:32-35`). With no secret, anyone who can reach `/webhook/github` can forge a push payload and trigger tweets. **Always set `WEBHOOK_SECRET`** (and note that webhook *creation* via `createWebhook` already refuses to proceed without one — `server.js:438`). With a secret set, signatures are compared with `crypto.timingSafeEqual`.

 succeeded in 762ms:
docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:5:GitLogs turns a `git push` into a published changelog tweet. A developer signs in with GitHub, picks a repository, and GitLogs installs a `push` webhook on it. From then on, every push fires `POST /webhook/github`; the backend verifies the GitHub HMAC signature, resolves which user owns the repo, and for each non-merge commit runs a two-stage AI pipeline — Stage 1 fetches the real commit diff from the GitHub REST API and asks Gemini to summarize it factually; Stage 2 feeds that grounded summary into the user's prompt template (AI-expanded only if the template contains `{{AI_TEXT}}`) to produce tweet text. The text is posted to the developer's own X account via OAuth 2.0 PKCE, optionally quoting a pinned "OG" tweet, and the resulting tweet ID is persisted. The Stage-2 changelog generation runs through a rate-limited, retrying, restart-survivable queue backed by SQLite (sql.js); note that the Stage-1 diff analysis calls Gemini directly and is **not** queued (a known weakness — see Failure modes). The whole thing is a single Node/Express process serving a React/Vite SPA from `frontend/dist`.
docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:67:        Note over WH: fails OPEN — verification skipped (known weakness)
docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:255:## Failure modes & known weaknesses
docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:257:- **HMAC fails OPEN when no secret is configured.** `verifyGitHubSignature` returns `true` (and only logs a warning) if neither a per-repo secret nor `WEBHOOK_SECRET` is set (`webhookHandler.js:32-35`). With no secret, anyone who can reach `/webhook/github` can forge a push payload and trigger tweets. **Always set `WEBHOOK_SECRET`** (and note that webhook *creation* via `createWebhook` already refuses to proceed without one — `server.js:438`). With a secret set, signatures are compared with `crypto.timingSafeEqual`.
README.md:56:    WH->>WH: HMAC-SHA256 verify (timingSafeEqual; fail CLOSED if no secret)
README.md:118:- **Webhook secret** — `WEBHOOK_SECRET`. **Do not skip this.** Signature verification fails *closed*: with no secret configured, every incoming webhook is rejected rather than trusted. Generate one with `openssl rand -hex 20`.
README.md:152:A single Express process serves the React SPA, terminates both OAuth flows, verifies and processes webhooks, and persists everything to a single-file sql.js database. Full component map, sequence diagrams, ER model, and a candid list of known weaknesses live in [`docs/ARCHITECTURE.md`](docs/ARCHITECTURE.md).
RUNBOOK.md:70:WEBHOOK_SECRET=<openssl rand -hex 20>   # REQUIRED — HMAC fails CLOSED without it

codex
**Findings**

- **P1: `/demo` is not keyless/offline.** [App.jsx](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/App.jsx:14) renders `Header` on every route, [Header.jsx](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/components/Header.jsx:16) calls `getCurrentUser()` on `/demo`, and [api.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/utils/api.js:19) computes `API_BASE` at module load. That directly contradicts [RUNBOOK.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/RUNBOOK.md:166) and [demoData.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/demo/demoData.js:10). A static `/demo` deploy still phones a backend or placeholder `/api/me`, and with missing `VITE_API_BASE` the production bundle can fail before routing. Isolate demo from the auth shell/API module or skip auth bootstrapping on `/demo`.

- **P1: The “generated” demo is canned output, not a pipeline.** [Demo.jsx](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/pages/Demo.jsx:182) renders `persona.thread`; [demoData.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/demo/demoData.js:98) hardcodes the tweet text. Yet [README.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/README.md:17) says prompt becomes a generated changelog post and [README.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/README.md:30) calls it “real generated.” This is product misrepresentation and will drift from the backend generator. Rename it as canned fixtures or run a real deterministic local generator.

- **P2: Security docs contradict each other.** README/runbook now claim webhook verification fails closed, but [docs/ARCHITECTURE.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:67) and [docs/ARCHITECTURE.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/docs/ARCHITECTURE.md:257) still say HMAC fails open. The code at [webhookHandler.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/src/webhookHandler.js:32) fails closed, so the architecture doc is stale. Do not ship security documentation that says the opposite of the implementation.

- **P2: Deployment runbook points production at dead infrastructure.** [deploy-ec2.yml](C:/Repo/gitlogs/.github/workflows/deploy-ec2.yml:29) defaults `VITE_API_BASE` to `https://api-gitlogs.aayushman.dev`, while [RUNBOOK.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/RUNBOOK.md:154) says that host is NXDOMAIN. The runbook says “set `VITE_API_BASE` in the deploy environment” at [RUNBOOK.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/RUNBOOK.md:142), but the workflow does not expose it as a required secret/env. Result: default deploy builds a broken SPA.

- **P2: Mobile persona selector will overflow.** [styles.css](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/styles.css:2484) makes `.demo-personas` a single nowrap flex row, and [styles.css](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/styles.css:2704) only changes the pipeline/toolbar at mobile widths. “Deadpan Technical” plus the other buttons will not fit on narrow phones. Add wrapping, full-width layout, or a real select/segmented control variant.

- **P2: ARIA roles are decorative but incomplete.** [Demo.jsx](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/pages/Demo.jsx:111) uses `tablist`/`tab`; [Demo.jsx](C:/Repo/gitlogs/frontend/src/pages/Demo.jsx:126) uses `radiogroup`/`radio`. There is no roving keyboard behavior, no `aria-controls`, no tabpanel relation, no arrow-key support. Either implement the semantics or remove the fake roles and use plain buttons/native radio inputs.

- **P3: README API table is incomplete after the rewrite.** It lists `GET /api/me/templates` at [README.md](C:/Repo/gitlogs/README.md:137), but omits the mutating template routes, `DELETE /api/me/templates/:templateId`, `/api/me/x/disconnect`, and `/api/me/repos/og-post` that exist in [server.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/src/server.js:586), [server.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/src/server.js:646), [server.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/src/server.js:806), and [server.js](C:/Repo/gitlogs/src/server.js:512). Public API docs that are selectively incomplete are maintenance debt.

**Test Gap**

No frontend tests cover `/demo`, persona switching, “no backend request on demo,” thread length limits, or mobile layout. I also could not run the frontend build in this sandbox because command startup failed with `windows sandbox: spawn setup refresh`.
